materials = multipass_materials		StructInt async = 0	}$		:i $GetArraySize$~%GLOBAL%$materials$	:i $material_array_size$ = %GLOBAL%$array_size$	:i $material_index$ = %i(0)	:i if (%GLOBAL%$material_array_size$ > %i(0))		:i while 		:i $material_name$ = (~%GLOBAL%$materials$:a{%GLOBAL%$material_index$:a}->$name$)		:i $GetArraySize$(~%GLOBAL%$materials$:a{%GLOBAL%$material_index$:a}->$pass$)		:i $pass_index$ = %i(0)		:i while 		:i $material_pass$ = (~%GLOBAL%$materials$:a{%GLOBAL%$material_index$:a}->$pass$:a{%GLOBAL%$pass_index$:a})		:i if (%GLOBAL%$pass_index$ = %i(0))			:i $material_name_pass$ = %GLOBAL%$material_name$		:i else 			:i $FormatText$$textname$ = $pass_text$%s("_pass%p")$p$ = (%GLOBAL%$pass_index$ + %i(1))			:i $extendcrc$%GLOBAL%$material_name$%GLOBAL%$pass_text$$out$ = $material_name_pass$		:i endif		:i if NOT $create_materials_from_list$$materials$ = $ingame_materials$$material_to_clone$ = %GLOBAL%$material_pass$$cloned_material_name$ = %GLOBAL%$material_name_pass$$async$ = %i(0)			:i $create_materials_from_list$$materials$ = $global_materials$$material_to_clone$ = %GLOBAL%$material_pass$$cloned_material_name$ = %GLOBAL%$material_name_pass$$async$ = %i(0)		:i endif		:i if NOT (%GLOBAL%$pass_index$ = %i(0))			:i $SetMaterialPass$$base$ = %GLOBAL%$material_name$$pass$ = %GLOBAL%$material_name_pass$		:i endif		:i %GLOBAL%$pass_index$ = (%GLOBAL%$pass_index$ + %i(1))		:i loop_to %GLOBAL%$array_size$		:i %GLOBAL%$material_index$ = (%GLOBAL%$material_index$ + %i(1))		:i $conditional_async_wait$$async$ = %GLOBAL%$async$		:i loop_to %GLOBAL%$material_array_size$	:i endif	:i endfunction]Script destroy_multipass_materials 0x5129eea8 [	${		StructQBKey materials = multipass_materials		StructInt async = 0	}$		:i $GetArraySize$~%GLOBAL%$materials$	:i $material_array_size$ = %GLOBAL%$array_size$	:i $material_index$ = %i(0)	:i if (%GLOBAL%$material_array_size$ > %i(0))		:i while 		:i $material_name$ = (~%GLOBAL%$materials$:a{%GLOBAL%$material_index$:a}->$name$)		:i $GetArraySize$(~%GLOBAL%$materials$:a{%GLOBAL%$material_index$:a}->$pass$)		:i $pass_index$ = %i(0)		:i while 		:i $material_pass$ = (~%GLOBAL%$materials$:a{%GLOBAL%$material_index$:a}->$pass$:a{%GLOBAL%$pass_index$:a})		:i if (%GLOBAL%$pass_index$ = %i(0))			:i $material_name_pass$ = %GLOBAL%$material_name$		:i else 			:i $FormatText$$textname$ = $pass_text$%s("_pass%p")$p$ = (%GLOBAL%$pass_index$ + %i(1))			:i $extendcrc$%GLOBAL%$material_name$%GLOBAL%$pass_text$$out$ = $material_name_pass$		:i endif		:i if NOT (%GLOBAL%$pass_index$ = %i(0))			:i $clearmaterialpass$$base$ = %GLOBAL%$material_name$$pass$ = %GLOBAL%$material_name_pass$			:i $DestroyMaterial$$name$ = %GLOBAL%$material_name_pass$		:i endif		:i %GLOBAL%$pass_index$ = (%GLOBAL%$pass_index$ + %i(1))		:i loop_to %GLOBAL%$array_size$		:i $DestroyMaterial$$name$ = %GLOBAL%$material_name$		:i %GLOBAL%$material_index$ = (%GLOBAL%$material_index$ + %i(1))		:i $conditional_async_wait$$async$ = %GLOBAL%$async$		:i loop_to %GLOBAL%$material_array_size$	:i endif	:i endfunction]
